\hypertarget{raygui_8h_source}{}\doxysection{raygui.\+h}
\label{raygui_8h_source}\index{include/external/raygui.h@{include/external/raygui.h}}
\mbox{\hyperlink{raygui_8h}{Go to the documentation of this file.}}
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{1 \textcolor{comment}{/*******************************************************************************************}}
\DoxyCodeLine{2 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui v3.2-\/dev -\/ A simple and easy-\/to-\/use immediate-\/mode gui library}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{5 \textcolor{comment}{*   DESCRIPTION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{6 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{7 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui is a tools-\/dev-\/focused immediate-\/mode-\/gui library based on raylib but also}}
\DoxyCodeLine{8 \textcolor{comment}{*   available as a standalone library, as long as input and drawing functions are provided.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{9 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{10 \textcolor{comment}{*   Controls provided:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{11 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{12 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Container/separators Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{13 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ WindowBox     -\/-\/> StatusBar, Panel}}
\DoxyCodeLine{14 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ GroupBox      -\/-\/> Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{15 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Line}}
\DoxyCodeLine{16 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Panel         -\/-\/> StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{17 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ScrollPanel   -\/-\/> StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{18 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{19 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Basic Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{20 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Label}}
\DoxyCodeLine{21 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{22 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ LabelButton   -\/-\/> Label}}
\DoxyCodeLine{23 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{24 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ToggleGroup   -\/-\/> Toggle}}
\DoxyCodeLine{25 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ CheckBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{26 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ComboBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{27 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ DropdownBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{28 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{29 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextBoxMulti}}
\DoxyCodeLine{30 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ValueBox      -\/-\/> TextBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{31 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Spinner       -\/-\/> Button, ValueBox}}
\DoxyCodeLine{32 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Slider}}
\DoxyCodeLine{33 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ SliderBar     -\/-\/> Slider}}
\DoxyCodeLine{34 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ProgressBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{35 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ StatusBar}}
\DoxyCodeLine{36 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ DummyRec}}
\DoxyCodeLine{37 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ Grid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{38 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{39 \textcolor{comment}{*   \# Advance Controls}}
\DoxyCodeLine{40 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ListView}}
\DoxyCodeLine{41 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ ColorPicker   -\/-\/> ColorPanel, ColorBarHue}}
\DoxyCodeLine{42 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ MessageBox    -\/-\/> Window, Label, Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{43 \textcolor{comment}{*       -\/ TextInputBox  -\/-\/> Window, Label, TextBox, Button}}
\DoxyCodeLine{44 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{45 \textcolor{comment}{*   It also provides a set of functions for styling the controls based on its properties (size, color).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{46 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{47 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{48 \textcolor{comment}{*   RAYGUI STYLE (guiStyle):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{49 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{50 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui uses a global data array for all gui style properties (allocated on data segment by default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{51 \textcolor{comment}{*   when a new style is loaded, it is loaded over the global style... but a default gui style could always be}}
\DoxyCodeLine{52 \textcolor{comment}{*   recovered with GuiLoadStyleDefault() function, that overwrites the current style to the default one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{53 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{54 \textcolor{comment}{*   The global style array size is fixed and depends on the number of controls and properties:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{55 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{56 \textcolor{comment}{*       static unsigned int guiStyle[RAYGUI\_MAX\_CONTROLS*(RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_BASE + RAYGUI\_MAX\_PROPS\_EXTENDED)];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{57 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{58 \textcolor{comment}{*   guiStyle size is by default: 16*(16 + 8) = 384*4 = 1536 bytes = 1.5 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{59 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{60 \textcolor{comment}{*   Note that the first set of BASE properties (by default guiStyle[0..15]) belong to the generic style}}
\DoxyCodeLine{61 \textcolor{comment}{*   used for all controls, when any of those base values is set, it is automatically populated to all}}
\DoxyCodeLine{62 \textcolor{comment}{*   controls, so, specific control values overwriting generic style should be set after base values.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{63 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{64 \textcolor{comment}{*   After the first BASE set we have the EXTENDED properties (by default guiStyle[16..23]), those}}
\DoxyCodeLine{65 \textcolor{comment}{*   properties are actually common to all controls and can not be overwritten individually (like BASE ones)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{66 \textcolor{comment}{*   Some of those properties are: TEXT\_SIZE, TEXT\_SPACING, LINE\_COLOR, BACKGROUND\_COLOR}}
\DoxyCodeLine{67 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{68 \textcolor{comment}{*   Custom control properties can be defined using the EXTENDED properties for each independent control.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{69 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{70 \textcolor{comment}{*   TOOL: rGuiStyler is a visual tool to customize raygui style.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{71 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{72 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{73 \textcolor{comment}{*   RAYGUI ICONS (guiIcons):}}
\DoxyCodeLine{74 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{75 \textcolor{comment}{*   raygui could use a global array containing icons data (allocated on data segment by default),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{76 \textcolor{comment}{*   a custom icons set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadIcons(), but loaded icons set}}
\DoxyCodeLine{77 \textcolor{comment}{*   must be same RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE and no more than RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS will be loaded}}
\DoxyCodeLine{78 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{79 \textcolor{comment}{*   Every icon is codified in binary form, using 1 bit per pixel, so, every 16x16 icon}}
\DoxyCodeLine{80 \textcolor{comment}{*   requires 8 integers (16*16/32) to be stored in memory.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{81 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{82 \textcolor{comment}{*   When the icon is draw, actually one quad per pixel is drawn if the bit for that pixel is set.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{83 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{84 \textcolor{comment}{*   The global icons array size is fixed and depends on the number of icons and size:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{85 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{86 \textcolor{comment}{*       static unsigned int guiIcons[RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS*RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS];}}
\DoxyCodeLine{87 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{88 \textcolor{comment}{*   guiIcons size is by default: 256*(16*16/32) = 2048*4 = 8192 bytes = 8 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{89 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{90 \textcolor{comment}{*   TOOL: rGuiIcons is a visual tool to customize raygui icons.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{91 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{92 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{93 \textcolor{comment}{*   CONFIGURATION:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{94 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{95 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_IMPLEMENTATION}}
\DoxyCodeLine{96 \textcolor{comment}{*       Generates the implementation of the library into the included file.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{97 \textcolor{comment}{*       If not defined, the library is in header only mode and can be included in other headers}}
\DoxyCodeLine{98 \textcolor{comment}{*       or source files without problems. But only ONE file should hold the implementation.}}
\DoxyCodeLine{99 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{100 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_STANDALONE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{101 \textcolor{comment}{*       Avoid raylib.h header inclusion in this file. Data types defined on raylib are defined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{102 \textcolor{comment}{*       internally in the library and input management and drawing functions must be provided by}}
\DoxyCodeLine{103 \textcolor{comment}{*       the user (check library implementation for further details).}}
\DoxyCodeLine{104 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{105 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_NO\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{106 \textcolor{comment}{*       Avoid including embedded ricons data (256 icons, 16x16 pixels, 1-\/bit per pixel, 2KB)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{107 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{108 \textcolor{comment}{*   \#define RAYGUI\_CUSTOM\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{109 \textcolor{comment}{*       Includes custom ricons.h header defining a set of custom icons,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{110 \textcolor{comment}{*       this file can be generated using rGuiIcons tool}}
\DoxyCodeLine{111 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{112 \textcolor{comment}{*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{113 \textcolor{comment}{*   VERSIONS HISTORY:}}

\DoxyCodeLine{205 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Microsoft specifiers to tell compiler that symbols are imported/exported from a .dll}}
\DoxyCodeLine{206 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#if defined(\_WIN32)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{207 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if defined(BUILD\_LIBTYPE\_SHARED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{208 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUIAPI \_\_declspec(dllexport)     }\textcolor{comment}{// We are building the library as a Win32 shared library (.dll)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{209 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#elif defined(USE\_LIBTYPE\_SHARED)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{210 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUIAPI \_\_declspec(dllimport)     }\textcolor{comment}{// We are using the library as a Win32 shared library (.dll)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{211 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{212 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#endif}}

\DoxyCodeLine{249 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#ifndef true}}
\DoxyCodeLine{250             \textcolor{keyword}{typedef} \textcolor{keyword}{enum} \{ \textcolor{keyword}{false}, \textcolor{keyword}{true} \} bool;}

\DoxyCodeLine{254     \textcolor{comment}{// Vector2 type}}

\DoxyCodeLine{263         \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} y;}

\DoxyCodeLine{852 \textcolor{comment}{// Embedded raygui icons, no external file provided}}
\DoxyCodeLine{853 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE               16       }\textcolor{comment}{// Size of icons (squared)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{854 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS         256       }\textcolor{comment}{// Maximum number of icons}}
\DoxyCodeLine{855 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_NAME\_LENGTH    32       }\textcolor{comment}{// Maximum length of icon name id}}
\DoxyCodeLine{856 }
\DoxyCodeLine{857 \textcolor{comment}{// Icons data is defined by bit array (every bit represents one pixel)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{858 \textcolor{comment}{// Those arrays are stored as unsigned int data arrays, so every array}}
\DoxyCodeLine{859 \textcolor{comment}{// element defines 32 pixels (bits) of information}}
\DoxyCodeLine{860 \textcolor{comment}{// Number of elemens depend on RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE (by default 16x16 pixels)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{861 \textcolor{preprocessor}{\#define RAYGUI\_ICON\_DATA\_ELEMENTS   (RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE*RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE/32)}}

\DoxyCodeLine{866 \textcolor{comment}{// Icons data for all gui possible icons (allocated on data segment by default)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{867 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{868 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 1: Every icon is codified in binary form, using 1 bit per pixel, so,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{869 \textcolor{comment}{// every 16x16 icon requires 8 integers (16*16/32) to be stored}}
\DoxyCodeLine{870 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{871 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 2: A different icon set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadIcons(),}}
\DoxyCodeLine{872 \textcolor{comment}{// but loaded icons set must be same RAYGUI\_ICON\_SIZE and no more than RAYGUI\_ICON\_MAX\_ICONS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{873 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{874 \textcolor{comment}{// guiIcons size is by default: 256*(16*16/32) = 2048*4 = 8192 bytes = 8 KB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{875 \textcolor{comment}{//-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1163 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 1: First set of BASE properties are generic to all controls but could be individually}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1165 \textcolor{comment}{// can not be overwritten individually but custom EXTENDED properties can be used by control}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1166 \textcolor{comment}{//}}
\DoxyCodeLine{1167 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE 2: A new style set could be loaded over this array using GuiLoadStyle(),}}

\DoxyCodeLine{1169 \textcolor{comment}{//}}

\DoxyCodeLine{3274             \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{3905 \textcolor{comment}{// Split controls text into multiple strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3906 \textcolor{comment}{// Also check for multiple columns (required by GuiToggleGroup())}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3907 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **GuiTextSplit(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *textRow)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3908 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3909     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Current implementation returns a copy of the provided string with '\(\backslash\)0' (string end delimiter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3910     \textcolor{comment}{// inserted between strings defined by "{}delimiter"{} parameter. No memory is dynamically allocated,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3911     \textcolor{comment}{// all used memory is static... it has some limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3912     \textcolor{comment}{//      1. Maximum number of possible split strings is set by RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3913     \textcolor{comment}{//      2. Maximum size of text to split is RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3914     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Those definitions could be externally provided if required}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3915 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3916 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3917 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS        128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3918 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3919 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3920 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE      1024}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3921 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3922 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3923     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *result[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS] = \{ NULL \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3924     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3925     memset(buffer, 0, RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{3926 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3927     result[0] = buffer;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3928     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} counter = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3929 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3930     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (textRow != NULL) textRow[0] = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3931 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3932     \textcolor{comment}{// Count how many substrings we have on text and point to every one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3933     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3934     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3935         buffer[i] = text[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3936         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3937         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{';'}) || (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{3938         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3939             result[counter] = buffer + i + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3940 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3941             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (textRow != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3942             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3943                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)n'}) textRow[counter] = textRow[counter -\/ 1] + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3944                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} textRow[counter] = textRow[counter -\/ 1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{3945             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3946 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3947             buffer[i] = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};   \textcolor{comment}{// Set an end of string at this point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3948 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3949             counter++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3950             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (counter == RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3951         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3952     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3953 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3954     *count = counter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3955 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3956     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3957 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3958 }

\DoxyCodeLine{3961 \textcolor{keyword}{static} Vector3 ConvertRGBtoHSV(Vector3 rgb)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3962 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3963     Vector3 hsv = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{3964     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} min = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3965     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} max = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3966     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} delta = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3967 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3968     min = (rgb.x < rgb.y)? rgb.x : rgb.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3969     min = (min < rgb.z)? min  : rgb.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3970 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3971     max = (rgb.x > rgb.y)? rgb.x : rgb.y;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3972     max = (max > rgb.z)? max  : rgb.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3973 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3974     hsv.z = max;            \textcolor{comment}{// Value}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3975     delta = max -\/ min;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3976 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3977     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (delta < 0.00001f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3978     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3979         hsv.y = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3980         hsv.x = 0.0f;           \textcolor{comment}{// Undefined, maybe NAN?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3981         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3982     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3983 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3984     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (max > 0.0f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{3985     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3986         \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If max is 0, this divide would cause a crash}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3987         hsv.y = (delta/max);    \textcolor{comment}{// Saturation}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3988     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3989     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3990     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{3991         \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: If max is 0, then r = g = b = 0, s = 0, h is undefined}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3992         hsv.y = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3993         hsv.x = 0.0f;           \textcolor{comment}{// Undefined, maybe NAN?}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3994         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{3995     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3996 }
\DoxyCodeLine{3997     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Comparing float values could not work properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3998     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgb.x >= max) hsv.x = (rgb.y -\/ rgb.z)/delta;    \textcolor{comment}{// Between yellow \& magenta}}
\DoxyCodeLine{3999     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4000     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4001         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (rgb.y >= max) hsv.x = 2.0f + (rgb.z -\/ rgb.x)/delta;  \textcolor{comment}{// Between cyan \& yellow}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4002         \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} hsv.x = 4.0f + (rgb.x -\/ rgb.y)/delta;      \textcolor{comment}{// Between magenta \& cyan}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4003     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4004 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4005     hsv.x *= 60.0f;     \textcolor{comment}{// Convert to degrees}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4006 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4007     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hsv.x < 0.0f) hsv.x += 360.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4008 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4009     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} hsv;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4010 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4011 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4012 \textcolor{comment}{// Convert color data from HSV to RGB}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4013 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Color data should be passed normalized}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4014 \textcolor{keyword}{static} Vector3 ConvertHSVtoRGB(Vector3 hsv)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4015 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4016     Vector3 rgb = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4017     \textcolor{keywordtype}{float} hh = 0.0f, p = 0.0f, q = 0.0f, t = 0.0f, ff = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4018     \textcolor{keywordtype}{long} i = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4019 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4020     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Comparing float values could not work properly}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4021     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hsv.y <= 0.0f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4022     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4023         rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4024         rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4025         rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4026         \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} rgb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4027     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4028 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4029     hh = hsv.x;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4030     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (hh >= 360.0f) hh = 0.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4031     hh /= 60.0f;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4032 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4033     i = (long)hh;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4034     ff = hh -\/ i;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4035     p = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ hsv.y);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4036     q = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ (hsv.y*ff));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4037     t = hsv.z*(1.0f -\/ (hsv.y*(1.0f -\/ ff)));}
\DoxyCodeLine{4038 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4039     \textcolor{keywordflow}{switch} (i)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4040     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4041         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 0:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4042         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4043             rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4044             rgb.y = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4045             rgb.z = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4046         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4047         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 1:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4048         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4049             rgb.x = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4050             rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4051             rgb.z = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4052         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4053         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 2:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4054         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4055             rgb.x = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4056             rgb.y = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4057             rgb.z = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4058         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4059         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 3:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4060         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4061             rgb.x = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4062             rgb.y = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4063             rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4064         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4065         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 4:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4066         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4067             rgb.x = t;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4068             rgb.y = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4069             rgb.z = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4070         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4071         \textcolor{keywordflow}{case} 5:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4072         \textcolor{keywordflow}{default}:}
\DoxyCodeLine{4073         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4074             rgb.x = hsv.z;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4075             rgb.y = p;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4076             rgb.z = q;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4077         \} \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4078     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4079 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4080     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} rgb;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4081 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4082 }

\DoxyCodeLine{4265 \textcolor{comment}{// Split string into multiple strings}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4266 \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} **TextSplit(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} delimiter, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *count)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4267 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4268     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: Current implementation returns a copy of the provided string with '\(\backslash\)0' (string end delimiter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4269     \textcolor{comment}{// inserted between strings defined by "{}delimiter"{} parameter. No memory is dynamically allocated,}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4270     \textcolor{comment}{// all used memory is static... it has some limitations:}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4271     \textcolor{comment}{//      1. Maximum number of possible split strings is set by RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4272     \textcolor{comment}{//      2. Maximum size of text to split is RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4273 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4274 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4275 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS        128}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4276 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4277 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#if !defined(RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4278 \textcolor{preprocessor}{        \#define RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE      1024}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4279 \textcolor{preprocessor}{    \#endif}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4280 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4281     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *result[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS] = \{ NULL \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4282     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} buffer[RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4283     memset(buffer, 0, RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4284 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4285     result[0] = buffer;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4286     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} counter = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4287 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4288     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (text != NULL)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4289     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4290         counter = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4291 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4292         \textcolor{comment}{// Count how many substrings we have on text and point to every one}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4293         \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; i < RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_TEXT\_SIZE; i++)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4294         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4295             buffer[i] = text[i];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4296             \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4297             \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (buffer[i] == delimiter)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4298             \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4299                 buffer[i] = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};   \textcolor{comment}{// Set an end of string at this point}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4300                 result[counter] = buffer + i + 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4301                 counter++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4302 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4303                 \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (counter == RAYGUI\_TEXTSPLIT\_MAX\_ITEMS) \textcolor{keywordflow}{break};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4304             \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4305         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4306     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4307 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4308     *count = counter;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4309     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} result;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4310 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4311 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4312 \textcolor{comment}{// Get integer value from text}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4313 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: This function replaces atoi() [stdlib.h]}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4314 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} TextToInteger(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4315 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4316     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} value = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4317     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} sign = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4318 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4319     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'+'}) || (text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4320     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4321         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (text[0] == \textcolor{charliteral}{'-\/'}) sign = -\/1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4322         text++;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4323     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4324 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4325     \textcolor{keywordflow}{for} (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} i = 0; ((text[i] >= \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'}) \&\& (text[i] <= \textcolor{charliteral}{'9'})); ++i) value = value*10 + (\textcolor{keywordtype}{int})(text[i] -\/ \textcolor{charliteral}{'0'});}
\DoxyCodeLine{4326 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4327     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} value*sign;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4328 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4329 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4330 \textcolor{comment}{// Encode codepoint into UTF-\/8 text (char array size returned as parameter)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4331 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *CodepointToUTF8(\textcolor{keywordtype}{int} codepoint, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *byteSize)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4332 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4333     \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} utf8[6] = \{ 0 \};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4334     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} size = 0;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4335 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4336     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x7f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4337     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4338         utf8[0] = (char)codepoint;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4339         size = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4340     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4341     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x7ff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4342     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4343         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 6) \& 0x1f) | 0xc0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4344         utf8[1] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4345         size = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4346     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4347     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0xffff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4348     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4349         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 12) \& 0x0f) | 0xe0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4350         utf8[1] = (char)(((codepoint >>  6) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4351         utf8[2] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4352         size = 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4353     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4354     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (codepoint <= 0x10ffff)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4355     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4356         utf8[0] = (char)(((codepoint >> 18) \& 0x07) | 0xf0);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4357         utf8[1] = (char)(((codepoint >> 12) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4358         utf8[2] = (char)(((codepoint >>  6) \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4359         utf8[3] = (char)((codepoint \& 0x3f) | 0x80);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4360         size = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4361     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4362 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4363     *byteSize = size;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4364 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4365     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} utf8;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4366 \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4367 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4368 \textcolor{comment}{// Get next codepoint in a UTF-\/8 encoded text, scanning until '\(\backslash\)0' is found}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4369 \textcolor{comment}{// When a invalid UTF-\/8 byte is encountered we exit as soon as possible and a '?'(0x3f) codepoint is returned}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4370 \textcolor{comment}{// Total number of bytes processed are returned as a parameter}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4371 \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: the standard says U+FFFD should be returned in case of errors}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4372 \textcolor{comment}{// but that character is not supported by the default font in raylib}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4373 \textcolor{keyword}{static} \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} GetCodepoint(\textcolor{keyword}{const} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} *text, \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} *bytesProcessed)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4374 \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4375 \textcolor{comment}{/*}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4376 \textcolor{comment}{    UTF-\/8 specs from https://www.ietf.org/rfc/rfc3629.txt}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4377 \textcolor{comment}{}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4378 \textcolor{comment}{    Char. number range  |        UTF-\/8 octet sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4379 \textcolor{comment}{      (hexadecimal)    |              (binary)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4380 \textcolor{comment}{    -\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/+-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/-\/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4381 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0000-\/0000 007F | 0xxxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4382 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0080-\/0000 07FF | 110xxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4383 \textcolor{comment}{    0000 0800-\/0000 FFFF | 1110xxxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4384 \textcolor{comment}{    0001 0000-\/0010 FFFF | 11110xxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx 10xxxxxx}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4385 \textcolor{comment}{*/}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4386     \textcolor{comment}{// NOTE: on decode errors we return as soon as possible}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4387 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4388     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} code = 0x3f;   \textcolor{comment}{// Codepoint (defaults to '?')}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4389     \textcolor{keywordtype}{int} octet = (\textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} char)(text[0]); \textcolor{comment}{// The first UTF8 octet}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4390     *bytesProcessed = 1;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4391 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4392     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet <= 0x7f)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4393     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4394         \textcolor{comment}{// Only one octet (ASCII range x00-\/7F)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4395         code = text[0];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4396     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4397     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xe0) == 0xc0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4398     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4399         \textcolor{comment}{// Two octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4400 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4401         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xC2-\/DF    [1]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4402         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4403 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4404         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4405 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4406         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet >= 0xc2) \&\& (octet <= 0xdf))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4407         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4408             code = ((octet \& 0x1f) << 6) | (octet1 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4409             *bytesProcessed = 2;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4410         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4411     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4412     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xf0) == 0xe0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4413     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4414         \textcolor{comment}{// Three octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4415         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4416         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet2 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4417 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4418         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4419 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4420         octet2 = text[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4421 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4422         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet2 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet2 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 3; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4423 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4424         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xE0    [1]xA0-\/BF       [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4425         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xE1-\/EC [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4426         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xED    [1]x80-\/9F       [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4427         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xEE-\/EF [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail(x80-\/BF)}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4428 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4429         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((octet == 0xe0) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0xa0) \&\& (octet1 <= 0xbf))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4430             ((octet == 0xed) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x80) \&\& (octet1 <= 0x9f)))) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4431 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4432         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet >= 0xe0) \&\& (0 <= 0xef))}
\DoxyCodeLine{4433         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4434             code = ((octet \& 0xf) << 12) | ((octet1 \& 0x3f) << 6) | (octet2 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4435             *bytesProcessed = 3;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4436         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4437     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4438     \textcolor{keywordflow}{else} \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet \& 0xf8) == 0xf0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4439     \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4440         \textcolor{comment}{// Four octets}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4441         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet > 0xf4) \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4442 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4443         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet1 = text[1];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4444         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet2 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4445         \textcolor{keywordtype}{unsigned} \textcolor{keywordtype}{char} octet3 = \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'};}
\DoxyCodeLine{4446 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4447         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet1 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet1 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4448 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4449         octet2 = text[2];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4450 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4451         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet2 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet2 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 3; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4452 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4453         octet3 = text[3];}
\DoxyCodeLine{4454 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4455         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} ((octet3 == \textcolor{charliteral}{'\(\backslash\)0'}) || ((octet3 >> 6) != 2)) \{ *bytesProcessed = 4; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \}  \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4456 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4457         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF0       [1]x90-\/BF       [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4458         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF1-\/F3    [1]UTF8-\/tail    [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4459         \textcolor{comment}{// [0]xF4       [1]x80-\/8F       [2]UTF8-\/tail  [3]UTF8-\/tail}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4460 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4461         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (((octet == 0xf0) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x90) \&\& (octet1 <= 0xbf))) ||}
\DoxyCodeLine{4462             ((octet == 0xf4) \&\& !((octet1 >= 0x80) \&\& (octet1 <= 0x8f)))) \{ *bytesProcessed = 2; \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code; \} \textcolor{comment}{// Unexpected sequence}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4463 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4464         \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (octet >= 0xf0)}
\DoxyCodeLine{4465         \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{4466             code = ((octet \& 0x7) << 18) | ((octet1 \& 0x3f) << 12) | ((octet2 \& 0x3f) << 6) | (octet3 \& 0x3f);}
\DoxyCodeLine{4467             *bytesProcessed = 4;}
\DoxyCodeLine{4468         \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4469     \}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4470 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4471     \textcolor{keywordflow}{if} (code > 0x10ffff) code = 0x3f;     \textcolor{comment}{// Codepoints after U+10ffff are invalid}}
\DoxyCodeLine{4472 }
\DoxyCodeLine{4473     \textcolor{keywordflow}{return} code;}
